+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_in_tile = tid // 2
+            chunk = tid % 2
+            global_row = block_row + row_in_tile
+            global_col = k_base + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * IN_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            row_warp = row_in_tile // 32
+            row_local = row_in_tile % 32
+            if chunk == 0:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i] = vals[i + 4]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i + 4] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i + 4] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            k_row = b_tid // 8
+            chunk = b_tid % 8
+            global_row = k_base + k_row
+            global_col = block_col + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * OUT_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            col_warp = chunk // 4
+            chunk_local = (chunk % 4) * 8
+            if k_row < 4:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 8:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 12:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 8] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.view(a_data[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        b_words = S.view(b_data[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS[col], S.f32)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)

+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            col_warp = chunk // 4
+            chunk_local = (chunk % 4) * 8
+            if k_row < 4:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 8:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 12:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 8] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.view(a_data[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        b_words = S.view(b_data[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS[col], S.f32)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)
+

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_epilogue():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_in_tile = tid // 2
+            chunk = tid % 2
+            global_row = block_row + row_in_tile
+            global_col = k_base + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * IN_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            row_warp = row_in_tile // 32
+            row_local = row_in_tile % 32
+            if chunk == 0:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i] = vals[i + 4]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i + 4] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i + 4] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            k_row = b_tid // 8
+            chunk = b_tid % 8
+            global_row = k_base + k_row
+            global_col = block_col + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * OUT_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            col_warp = chunk // 4
+            chunk_local = (chunk % 4) * 8
+            if k_row < 4:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 8:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 12:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 8] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.view(a_data[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        b_words = S.view(b_data[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS[col], S.f32)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)

+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK

+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2

+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+def _launch_epilogue():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_in_tile = tid // 2
+            chunk = tid % 2
+            global_row = block_row + row_in_tile
+            global_col = k_base + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * IN_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            row_warp = row_in_tile // 32
+            row_local = row_in_tile % 32
+            if chunk == 0:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i] = vals[i + 4]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i + 4] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i + 4] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            k_row = b_tid // 8
+            chunk = b_tid % 8
+            global_row = k_base + k_row
+            global_col = block_col + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * OUT_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            col_warp = chunk // 4
+            chunk_local = (chunk % 4) * 8
+            if k_row < 4:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 8:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 12:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 8] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.view(a_data[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        b_words = S.view(b_data[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS[col], S.f32)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)

+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_in_tile = tid // 2
+            chunk = tid % 2
+            global_row = block_row + row_in_tile
+            global_col = k_base + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * IN_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            row_warp = row_in_tile // 32
+            row_local = row_in_tile % 32
+            if chunk == 0:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i] = vals[i + 4]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i + 4] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i + 4] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            k_row = b_tid // 8
+            chunk = b_tid % 8
+            global_row = k_base + k_row
+            global_col = block_col + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * OUT_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            col_warp = chunk // 4
+            chunk_local = (chunk % 4) * 8
+            if k_row < 4:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 8:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 12:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 8] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.view(a_data[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        b_words = S.view(b_data[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS[col], S.f32)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)
+
+

The remaining error is small enough that reduction order can matter. I’m replacing the tree reduction in the groupnorm block with a single-thread exact 32-element accumulation that matches the original algorithm’s order, then I’ll rerun the same harness command.

+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK

+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2

+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+def _launch_epilogue():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_epilogue():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_in_tile = tid // 2
+            chunk = tid % 2
+            global_row = block_row + row_in_tile
+            global_col = k_base + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * IN_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            row_warp = row_in_tile // 32
+            row_local = row_in_tile % 32
+            if chunk == 0:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i] = vals[i + 4]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i + 4] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i + 4] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            k_row = b_tid // 8
+            chunk = b_tid % 8
+            global_row = k_base + k_row
+            global_col = block_col + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * OUT_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            col_warp = chunk // 4
+            chunk_local = (chunk % 4) * 8
+            if k_row < 4:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 8:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 12:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 8] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.view(a_data[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        b_words = S.view(b_data[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS[col], S.f32)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_epilogue():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_in_tile = tid // 2
+            chunk = tid % 2
+            global_row = block_row + row_in_tile
+            global_col = k_base + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * IN_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            row_warp = row_in_tile // 32
+            row_local = row_in_tile % 32
+            if chunk == 0:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i] = vals[i + 4]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i + 4] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i + 4] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            k_row = b_tid // 8
+            chunk = b_tid % 8
+            global_row = k_base + k_row
+            global_col = block_col + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * OUT_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            col_warp = chunk // 4
+            chunk_local = (chunk % 4) * 8
+            if k_row < 4:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 8:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 12:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 8] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.view(a_data[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        b_words = S.view(b_data[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS[col], S.f32)
+

+        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_epilogue():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))
+

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_in_tile = tid // 2
+            chunk = tid % 2
+            global_row = block_row + row_in_tile
+            global_col = k_base + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * IN_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            row_warp = row_in_tile // 32
+            row_local = row_in_tile % 32
+            if chunk == 0:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i] = vals[i + 4]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i + 4] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i + 4] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            k_row = b_tid // 8
+            chunk = b_tid % 8
+            global_row = k_base + k_row
+            global_col = block_col + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * OUT_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            col_warp = chunk // 4
+            chunk_local = (chunk % 4) * 8
+            if k_row < 4:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 8:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 12:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 8] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.view(a_data[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        b_words = S.view(b_data[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS[col], S.f32)
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)
+

codex
The last residual looks like parameter-dtype drift rather than tile math. I’m keeping the MFMA weight path in bf16, but moving bias, groupnorm weights/bias, and the multiply weight back to fp32 inside the substrate kernels to better match the reference module semantics.
apply patch

+            global_col = block_col + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * OUT_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            col_warp = chunk // 4
+            chunk_local = (chunk % 4) * 8
+            if k_row < 4:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 8:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 12:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 8] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.view(a_data[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        b_words = S.view(b_data[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = BIAS[col]
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_epilogue():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_in_tile = tid // 2
+            chunk = tid % 2
+            global_row = block_row + row_in_tile
+            global_col = k_base + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * IN_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            row_warp = row_in_tile // 32
+            row_local = row_in_tile % 32
+            if chunk == 0:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i] = vals[i + 4]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i + 4] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i + 4] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            k_row = b_tid // 8
+            chunk = b_tid % 8
+            global_row = k_base + k_row
+            global_col = block_col + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * OUT_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            col_warp = chunk // 4
+            chunk_local = (chunk % 4) * 8
+            if k_row < 4:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 8:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 12:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 8] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.view(a_data[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        b_words = S.view(b_data[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = BIAS[col]
+

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_epilogue():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_in_tile = tid // 2
+            chunk = tid % 2
+            global_row = block_row + row_in_tile
+            global_col = k_base + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * IN_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            row_warp = row_in_tile // 32
+            row_local = row_in_tile % 32
+            if chunk == 0:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i] = vals[i + 4]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i + 4] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i + 4] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            k_row = b_tid // 8
+            chunk = b_tid % 8
+            global_row = k_base + k_row
+            global_col = block_col + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * OUT_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            col_warp = chunk // 4
+            chunk_local = (chunk % 4) * 8
+            if k_row < 4:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 8:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 12:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 8] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.view(a_data[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        b_words = S.view(b_data[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = BIAS[col]
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)
+

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_epilogue():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_in_tile = tid // 2
+            chunk = tid % 2
+            global_row = block_row + row_in_tile
+            global_col = k_base + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * IN_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            row_warp = row_in_tile // 32
+            row_local = row_in_tile % 32
+            if chunk == 0:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i] = vals[i + 4]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i + 4] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i + 4] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            k_row = b_tid // 8
+            chunk = b_tid % 8
+            global_row = k_base + k_row
+            global_col = block_col + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * OUT_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            col_warp = chunk // 4
+            chunk_local = (chunk % 4) * 8
+            if k_row < 4:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 8:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 12:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 8] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.view(a_data[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        b_words = S.view(b_data[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = BIAS[col]
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)

I’m making one last precision-alignment change in the epilogue: quantizing the sigmoid outputs themselves to bf16 before the multiplies. The current error is already down at a single bf16 step, so this is the most plausible remaining source.

+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+
+def _launch_epilogue():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_in_tile = tid // 2
+            chunk = tid % 2
+            global_row = block_row + row_in_tile
+            global_col = k_base + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * IN_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            row_warp = row_in_tile // 32
+            row_local = row_in_tile % 32
+            if chunk == 0:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i] = vals[i + 4]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i + 4] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i + 4] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            k_row = b_tid // 8
+            chunk = b_tid % 8
+            global_row = k_base + k_row
+            global_col = block_col + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * OUT_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            col_warp = chunk // 4
+            chunk_local = (chunk % 4) * 8
+            if k_row < 4:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 8:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 12:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 8] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.view(a_data[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        b_words = S.view(b_data[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = BIAS[col]
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)
+
+

+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2

+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+def _launch_epilogue():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_in_tile = tid // 2
+            chunk = tid % 2
+            global_row = block_row + row_in_tile
+            global_col = k_base + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * IN_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            row_warp = row_in_tile // 32
+            row_local = row_in_tile % 32
+            if chunk == 0:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i] = vals[i + 4]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i + 4] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i + 4] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            k_row = b_tid // 8
+            chunk = b_tid % 8
+            global_row = k_base + k_row
+            global_col = block_col + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * OUT_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            col_warp = chunk // 4
+            chunk_local = (chunk % 4) * 8
+            if k_row < 4:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 8:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 12:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 8] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.view(a_data[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        b_words = S.view(b_data[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = BIAS[col]
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)
+

+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_in_tile = tid // 2
+            chunk = tid % 2
+            global_row = block_row + row_in_tile
+            global_col = k_base + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * IN_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            row_warp = row_in_tile // 32
+            row_local = row_in_tile % 32
+            if chunk == 0:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i] = vals[i + 4]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i + 4] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i + 4] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            k_row = b_tid // 8
+            chunk = b_tid % 8
+            global_row = k_base + k_row
+            global_col = block_col + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * OUT_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            col_warp = chunk // 4
+            chunk_local = (chunk % 4) * 8
+            if k_row < 4:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 8:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 12:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 8] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.view(a_data[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        b_words = S.view(b_data[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = BIAS[col]
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)

 GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_epilogue():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))
+

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_data = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            row_in_tile = tid // 2
+            chunk = tid % 2
+            global_row = block_row + row_in_tile
+            global_col = k_base + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * IN_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            row_warp = row_in_tile // 32
+            row_local = row_in_tile % 32
+            if chunk == 0:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i] = vals[i + 4]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(4):
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local, i + 4] = vals[i]
+                    a_data[row_warp, row_local + 32, i + 4] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            k_row = b_tid // 8
+            chunk = b_tid % 8
+            global_row = k_base + k_row
+            global_col = block_col + chunk * 8
+            offset = S.convert((global_row * OUT_FEATURES + global_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+            col_warp = chunk // 4
+            chunk_local = (chunk % 4) * 8
+            if k_row < 4:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 8:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            elif k_row < 12:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i, k_row - 4] = vals[i]
+            else:
+                for i in S.range(8):
+                    b_data[col_warp, chunk_local + i + 32, k_row - 8] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.view(a_data[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        b_words = S.view(b_data[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = BIAS[col]
+
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)
+
